## Chapter: Equity & Inclusion: Local Policy-Driven Strategies for Economic Development & the Just City":

### Introduction

In today's rapidly changing world, the concept of equity and inclusion has become a crucial aspect of urban planning and development. As cities continue to grow and evolve, it is essential to ensure that all members of the community have equal access to resources and opportunities. This includes addressing issues of social, economic, and environmental equity. In this chapter, we will explore the intersection of equity and inclusion in the context of urban planning and development. We will discuss the various factors that contribute to equity and inclusion, and how local policies can be used to promote and maintain these principles. By the end of this chapter, readers will have a better understanding of the importance of equity and inclusion in creating a just and sustainable city.


# Title: Equity & Inclusion: Local Policy-Driven Strategies for Economic Development & the Just City":

## Chapter 8: Equity & Inclusion in Urban Planning and Development:




### Introduction

In this chapter, we will explore the intersection of cultural heritage and preservation in the context of economic development and the just city. Cultural heritage and preservation are crucial components of a city's identity and can significantly influence its economic development. The preservation of cultural heritage can stimulate economic growth by attracting tourists, creating job opportunities, and fostering a sense of community pride. However, the process of preservation can also be complex and contentious, involving multiple stakeholders and competing interests.

We will delve into the various aspects of cultural heritage and preservation, including their definitions, importance, and the challenges they face. We will also examine the role of local policies in promoting and protecting cultural heritage and preservation. These policies can range from regulatory measures to incentivizing strategies, and their effectiveness will be assessed based on real-world examples.

Furthermore, we will discuss the concept of the just city and how cultural heritage and preservation contribute to its realization. The just city is a concept that aims to create a fair and equitable urban environment where all residents have equal access to opportunities and resources. Cultural heritage and preservation can play a significant role in achieving this goal by promoting diversity, inclusivity, and community engagement.

Overall, this chapter aims to provide a comprehensive understanding of the relationship between cultural heritage, preservation, and the just city. It will equip readers with the knowledge and tools to navigate the complexities of these topics and contribute to the creation of more inclusive and sustainable urban environments.




### Subsection: 8.1a Importance of Cultural Heritage

Cultural heritage is a fundamental aspect of a city's identity and plays a crucial role in its economic development. It encompasses the tangible and intangible aspects of a community's history, traditions, and values, and is often reflected in its architecture, art, and customs. Preserving and promoting cultural heritage can stimulate economic growth by attracting tourists, creating job opportunities, and fostering a sense of community pride.

#### Economic Benefits

The preservation of cultural heritage can have significant economic benefits. As mentioned in the previous chapter, the tourism industry is one of the largest industries in the world, and cultural heritage is a major draw for tourists. By preserving and promoting their cultural heritage, cities can attract more tourists, leading to increased revenue from tourism. This can also create job opportunities in the tourism sector, contributing to the local economy.

Moreover, the preservation of cultural heritage can also increase property values. As mentioned in the related context, the preservation of historic buildings can increase property values in the surrounding area. This can lead to increased tax revenue for the city, further contributing to its economic development.

#### Social and Cultural Benefits

Cultural heritage also plays a crucial role in fostering a sense of community pride and identity. By preserving and promoting their cultural heritage, communities can celebrate their unique history and traditions, fostering a sense of pride and belonging among its members. This can also lead to increased community engagement and participation, as community members come together to preserve and promote their cultural heritage.

Furthermore, cultural heritage can also contribute to social cohesion and understanding. By learning about and celebrating different cultural heritages, individuals can gain a deeper understanding and appreciation for diverse cultures, leading to increased social cohesion and understanding.

#### Challenges and Solutions

Despite its numerous benefits, preserving cultural heritage can also be a complex and contentious process. As mentioned in the related context, there can be competing interests and challenges in the preservation of cultural heritage. For example, the preservation of historic buildings may conflict with the need for modern development.

To address these challenges, local policies can play a crucial role. These policies can range from regulatory measures, such as preservation laws and guidelines, to incentivizing strategies, such as tax breaks for preserving historic buildings. By working closely with the community, these policies can be tailored to address the specific needs and concerns of the community, ensuring the preservation of cultural heritage while also promoting economic development.

In conclusion, cultural heritage is a crucial aspect of a city's identity and plays a significant role in its economic development. By understanding its importance and implementing effective local policies, cities can preserve and promote their cultural heritage, leading to increased economic growth, social cohesion, and community pride.





### Subsection: 8.1b Preservation Planning and Policies

Preservation planning and policies are crucial for the effective preservation of cultural heritage. These plans and policies provide a framework for decision-making and action, ensuring that preservation efforts are guided by a clear vision and strategy. They also help to ensure that preservation efforts are equitable and inclusive, addressing the needs and concerns of all members of the community.

#### Preservation Planning

Preservation planning involves the development of a strategy for preserving and promoting cultural heritage. This strategy should be based on a thorough understanding of the community's cultural heritage, including its tangible and intangible aspects. It should also take into account the community's needs and concerns, as well as its economic, social, and cultural context.

Preservation planning can be a complex and challenging process, requiring the involvement of a wide range of stakeholders, including community members, government agencies, and cultural institutions. However, it is essential for ensuring that preservation efforts are effective and sustainable.

#### Preservation Policies

Preservation policies provide a set of guidelines and standards for preservation efforts. These policies should be developed in consultation with the community and should be based on the principles of equity and inclusion. They should also take into account the community's cultural heritage, as well as its economic, social, and cultural context.

Preservation policies can cover a wide range of issues, including the preservation of historic buildings, the protection of cultural property, and the promotion of cultural diversity. They can also provide guidance on decision-making, helping to ensure that preservation efforts are guided by a clear vision and strategy.

#### Implementation and Monitoring

The implementation and monitoring of preservation planning and policies are crucial for their success. This involves the development of an action plan, which outlines the specific steps that will be taken to implement the preservation strategy. It also involves the establishment of a monitoring system, which can track progress and identify any issues that may arise.

The implementation and monitoring of preservation planning and policies should be an ongoing process, with regular reviews and updates as needed. This can help to ensure that preservation efforts are effective and sustainable, and that they continue to meet the needs and concerns of the community.

#### Conclusion

Preservation planning and policies are essential for the effective preservation of cultural heritage. They provide a framework for decision-making and action, ensuring that preservation efforts are guided by a clear vision and strategy. They also help to ensure that preservation efforts are equitable and inclusive, addressing the needs and concerns of all members of the community. The implementation and monitoring of these plans and policies are crucial for their success, and should be an ongoing process.




### Subsection: 8.1c Balancing Development and Preservation

Balancing development and preservation is a critical aspect of cultural heritage and preservation. As communities grow and evolve, they often face the challenge of balancing the need for development with the preservation of their cultural heritage. This balance is essential for maintaining the community's identity and sense of place, while also meeting the needs of its current and future residents.

#### The Importance of Balancing Development and Preservation

Balancing development and preservation is crucial for several reasons. First, it helps to maintain the community's cultural identity and sense of place. Cultural heritage is often deeply intertwined with the physical environment, and the loss of historic buildings, landscapes, or other cultural resources can result in the loss of the community's unique identity.

Second, it can contribute to economic development. Preservation efforts can stimulate tourism, attract investment, and create jobs. For example, the preservation of historic buildings can attract tourists, leading to increased revenue from tourism. Similarly, the preservation of cultural property can increase property values, attracting investment and creating jobs in the construction and real estate sectors.

Finally, it can help to address issues of equity and inclusion. Preservation efforts can help to ensure that all members of the community have access to and benefit from the community's cultural heritage. This can be particularly important for marginalized or disadvantaged groups, who may have a strong connection to certain aspects of the community's cultural heritage.

#### Strategies for Balancing Development and Preservation

Balancing development and preservation requires a careful and strategic approach. Here are some strategies that can be used:

- **Preservation by Design**: This strategy involves incorporating preservation considerations into the design and planning process. For example, when developing a new building or project, preservationists can work with architects and planners to ensure that the new development is compatible with and respectful of the surrounding cultural heritage.

- **Preservation Easements**: Preservation easements are legal agreements that restrict the use of a property in order to protect its cultural heritage. These easements can be used to protect historic buildings, landscapes, or other cultural resources from incompatible development.

- **Adaptive Reuse**: Adaptive reuse involves repurposing existing buildings for new uses. This strategy can help to preserve historic buildings while also meeting the needs of the community. For example, an old factory might be converted into a housing development or a community center.

- **Preservation Funding**: Preservation efforts often require funding, and this can be a challenge, especially in communities with limited resources. However, there are various sources of funding available, including government grants, private donations, and tax incentives.

In conclusion, balancing development and preservation is a complex but crucial task. It requires a careful and strategic approach, and it is essential for maintaining the community's cultural heritage, promoting economic development, and addressing issues of equity and inclusion.

### Conclusion

In conclusion, cultural heritage and preservation are integral components of local policy-driven strategies for economic development and the just city. The preservation of cultural heritage not only helps to maintain a community's identity and sense of place, but it also contributes to economic development by attracting tourists and stimulating local economies. Furthermore, cultural preservation can play a crucial role in promoting social cohesion and inclusivity, as it allows for the celebration and recognition of diverse cultural identities within a community. 

Local policies that prioritize cultural heritage and preservation can take various forms, including zoning regulations, tax incentives, and public funding. These policies can help to ensure that cultural heritage is protected and preserved, while also promoting economic development and social cohesion. 

However, it is important to note that cultural preservation is not without its challenges. These can include issues of ownership and control, as well as the potential for gentrification and displacement. Therefore, it is crucial for local policies to be developed in consultation with all stakeholders, and to be regularly reviewed and updated to address any emerging issues. 

In the end, cultural heritage and preservation are key to creating a just city that is both economically vibrant and socially inclusive. By prioritizing cultural preservation in local policies, we can help to ensure that our cities are places where all residents can thrive and where cultural diversity is valued and celebrated.

Research and write a brief report on a local policy that prioritizes cultural heritage and preservation. Discuss its objectives, strategies, and potential impacts.

#### Exercise 2
Imagine you are a city planner tasked with developing a new local policy for cultural preservation. Outline the key components of this policy, including any potential challenges and how you would address them.

#### Exercise 3

#### Exercise 4

## Chapter: Chapter 9: Public Art and Cultural Expression

### Introduction

Public art and cultural expression are integral components of a vibrant and inclusive city. They serve as a reflection of the community's identity, values, and aspirations, and can significantly contribute to the quality of life for its residents. This chapter will delve into the role of public art and cultural expression in local policy-driven strategies for economic development and the just city.

Public art, in its various forms, can transform urban spaces into dynamic and engaging environments. It can stimulate dialogue, provoke thought, and foster a sense of community. By integrating public art into local policies, cities can create a more inclusive and equitable environment for all residents, regardless of their socio-economic status or cultural background.

Cultural expression, on the other hand, refers to the ways in which individuals and communities express their cultural identity. This can include traditional practices, rituals, and festivals, as well as contemporary forms of expression such as music, dance, and visual arts. By promoting and protecting cultural expression, cities can foster a sense of belonging and pride among their residents, and contribute to a more cohesive and harmonious society.

In this chapter, we will explore the various ways in which public art and cultural expression can be integrated into local policies, and the potential benefits and challenges associated with this. We will also discuss case studies of cities that have successfully implemented such policies, and the lessons that can be learned from their experiences.

By the end of this chapter, readers should have a better understanding of the role of public art and cultural expression in local policy-driven strategies for economic development and the just city. They should also be equipped with the knowledge and tools to develop and implement such strategies in their own communities.




### Conclusion

In this chapter, we have explored the importance of cultural heritage and preservation in creating a just city. We have discussed how cultural heritage is a reflection of a community's identity and how it can contribute to economic development. We have also examined the various strategies that local governments can use to preserve and promote cultural heritage, such as creating cultural districts, implementing cultural preservation policies, and involving the community in the preservation process.

One of the key takeaways from this chapter is the importance of inclusivity in cultural preservation. By involving all members of the community in the preservation process, we can ensure that their voices are heard and their cultural heritage is respected. This not only promotes a sense of belonging and pride within the community, but also helps to create a more equitable and just city.

Another important aspect of cultural preservation is its role in promoting economic development. By preserving and promoting cultural heritage, we can attract tourists and create job opportunities in the cultural sector. This not only benefits the local economy, but also helps to preserve and celebrate the community's cultural identity.

In conclusion, cultural heritage and preservation are crucial components of creating a just city. By promoting inclusivity and economic development, we can ensure that all members of the community have a voice in preserving their cultural heritage and promoting a sense of pride and belonging.

# Title: Equity & Inclusion: Local Policy-Driven Strategies for Economic Development & the Just City":

## Chapter 9: Equity & Inclusion:




### Introduction

In this chapter, we will explore the intersection of arts planning and economic development, and how it contributes to creating a just city. The arts have long been recognized as a powerful tool for community building and revitalization, and their potential for economic development is immense. However, the relationship between the arts and economic development is often complex and multifaceted, requiring careful planning and policy-making to fully realize its potential.

We will begin by examining the role of the arts in economic development, exploring how they can stimulate local economies, create jobs, and attract investment. We will also discuss the challenges and opportunities that arise when incorporating the arts into economic development strategies, such as funding and community engagement.

Next, we will delve into the concept of arts planning, exploring how it can be used to guide and shape the development of the arts in a community. We will discuss the importance of involving diverse stakeholders in the planning process, and how arts planning can be used to address issues of equity and inclusion.

Finally, we will examine case studies of successful arts planning and economic development projects, highlighting the strategies and policies that were used and the outcomes that were achieved. These case studies will provide valuable insights and lessons learned for communities looking to incorporate the arts into their economic development plans.

By the end of this chapter, readers will have a comprehensive understanding of the role of the arts in economic development, the importance of arts planning, and the potential for the arts to contribute to creating a just city. They will also have the tools and knowledge to develop and implement effective arts planning and economic development strategies in their own communities.




### Section: 9.1 Arts Planning & Economic Development:

#### 9.1a The Role of the Arts in Urban Development

The arts play a crucial role in urban development, serving as a catalyst for economic growth and community revitalization. They have the power to transform public spaces, stimulate local economies, and create a sense of place and identity for a community. In this section, we will explore the various ways in which the arts contribute to urban development, and how they can be effectively integrated into economic development strategies.

#### 9.1b The Arts as a Catalyst for Economic Growth

The arts have been shown to have a significant impact on the local economy. According to the National Endowment for the Arts, the arts industry contributes over $700 billion to the U.S. economy, supporting over 4.8 million jobs. This includes jobs in the creative sector, such as artists, designers, and musicians, as well as jobs in related industries, such as tourism and hospitality.

In urban areas, the arts can serve as a magnet for economic development. By attracting visitors and residents to cultural events and attractions, the arts can stimulate local businesses and create job opportunities. For example, the High Line in New York City, a 1.45-mile-long elevated linear park built on a former railroad track, has become a popular tourist destination and has led to the development of new businesses and housing in the surrounding area.

#### 9.1c The Arts and Community Revitalization

The arts also play a crucial role in community revitalization. By transforming public spaces and creating a sense of place and identity, the arts can help to improve the quality of life for residents and attract new residents to a community. This can lead to increased property values and a more vibrant and thriving community.

In addition, the arts can serve as a tool for community engagement and empowerment. By involving residents in the creation and management of public art projects, communities can foster a sense of ownership and pride, leading to a stronger sense of community and social cohesion.

#### 9.1d The Arts and Equity & Inclusion

The arts have the potential to address issues of equity and inclusion in urban development. By providing opportunities for diverse voices and perspectives to be heard and represented, the arts can help to create a more inclusive and equitable society. This can be achieved through initiatives such as diversity training for arts organizations and funding for underrepresented artists.

In addition, the arts can serve as a platform for addressing social and political issues. By providing a space for dialogue and discussion, the arts can help to raise awareness and promote understanding of complex issues, leading to more inclusive and equitable communities.

#### 9.1e The Role of Arts Planning in Economic Development

Arts planning plays a crucial role in integrating the arts into economic development strategies. It involves the careful planning and management of arts and cultural resources to achieve specific economic and social goals. This can include identifying and prioritizing arts and cultural assets, developing policies and programs to support the arts, and collaborating with other stakeholders to leverage the arts for economic development.

In the next section, we will explore the various strategies and tools that can be used in arts planning for economic development.

#### 9.1b The Role of the Arts in Community Development

The arts play a crucial role in community development, serving as a powerful tool for creating a sense of place, fostering community engagement, and promoting social and economic well-being. In this section, we will explore the various ways in which the arts contribute to community development, and how they can be effectively integrated into community planning and policy-making.

##### The Arts as a Reflection of Community Identity

The arts have the unique ability to capture and express the essence of a community, serving as a reflection of its history, culture, and values. Through the creation and display of art, communities can showcase their identity and sense of place, attracting visitors and residents alike. For example, the city of Santa Fe, New Mexico, is known for its vibrant arts scene, which is deeply rooted in the city's history and cultural heritage. The city's commitment to preserving and promoting its artistic legacy has led to the development of a thriving arts industry, contributing to its economic growth and community identity.

##### The Arts as a Catalyst for Community Engagement

The arts also play a crucial role in community engagement, providing a platform for residents to express their ideas, share their stories, and connect with others. By involving residents in the creation and management of public art projects, communities can foster a sense of ownership and pride, leading to increased community participation and a stronger sense of community cohesion. For instance, the city of Portland, Oregon, has implemented a community-driven public art program, where residents are actively involved in the selection and creation of public artworks. This has not only resulted in a more vibrant and visually appealing city, but also a more engaged and connected community.

##### The Arts and Social and Economic Well-being

The arts have been shown to have a significant impact on social and economic well-being. By providing opportunities for education, employment, and social interaction, the arts can improve the quality of life for individuals and communities. For example, the city of Boston, Massachusetts, has implemented a comprehensive arts education program, providing access to high-quality arts education for all students. This has not only improved academic achievement, but also fostered creativity and critical thinking skills, contributing to the city's economic growth and social development.

In conclusion, the arts play a crucial role in community development, serving as a reflection of community identity, a catalyst for community engagement, and a contributor to social and economic well-being. By integrating the arts into community planning and policy-making, communities can create a more vibrant, inclusive, and sustainable future for all.

#### 9.1c Case Studies of Arts Planning in Economic Development

In this section, we will explore some case studies that highlight the role of arts planning in economic development. These case studies will provide real-world examples of how arts planning can be used to stimulate economic growth, create jobs, and enhance the quality of life in a community.

##### Case Study 1: The High Line, New York City

The High Line is a 1.45-mile-long elevated linear park built on a former railroad track in New York City. The project was initiated by a group of local residents who saw the potential of the abandoned railway as a public space for art, recreation, and community gathering. The High Line has become a popular tourist attraction, drawing over 8 million visitors each year. It has also led to the development of new businesses, such as restaurants, galleries, and hotels, creating jobs and stimulating economic growth in the surrounding neighborhood.

##### Case Study 2: The Creative District, Portland

The Creative District in Portland, Oregon, is a designated area where arts and culture play a central role in economic development. The district is home to a diverse range of creative businesses, including galleries, studios, and performance spaces. The district has been instrumental in attracting creative professionals to the area, leading to the creation of over 1,000 jobs. It has also contributed to the revitalization of the surrounding neighborhoods, with property values increasing by over 50% in the last decade.

##### Case Study 3: The Arts Education Program, Boston

The Arts Education Program in Boston, Massachusetts, is a comprehensive initiative that provides access to high-quality arts education for all students. The program has been shown to have a significant impact on academic achievement, with students who participate in the program showing improved test scores and graduation rates. The program has also led to the creation of new jobs in the arts sector, as well as increased community engagement and pride in the city's artistic legacy.

These case studies demonstrate the diverse ways in which arts planning can be used to drive economic development. By integrating the arts into community planning and policy-making, cities can create vibrant, inclusive, and sustainable communities that attract residents, visitors, and businesses, and contribute to the overall well-being of their residents.




### Conclusion

In this chapter, we have explored the role of arts planning in economic development and the just city. We have seen how the arts can serve as a catalyst for economic growth, community revitalization, and social inclusion. By incorporating arts planning into local policies and strategies, cities can create a more vibrant and equitable environment for all residents.

We have also discussed the importance of involving the community in the planning process, as well as the need for diversity and inclusivity in the arts. By promoting diversity and inclusivity, cities can create a more just and equitable society, where all residents have equal access to the arts and the benefits they bring.

As we have seen, the arts have the power to transform communities and bring people together. By utilizing arts planning as a tool for economic development and creating a more just city, we can create a better future for all.

## Chapter: Chapter 10: Public Art & Social Inclusion

### Introduction

In this chapter, we will explore the intersection of public art and social inclusion in the context of local policy-driven strategies for economic development and the just city. Public art, as a form of expression and communication, has the power to shape the social, cultural, and economic landscape of a city. It can serve as a tool for promoting social inclusion, by providing a platform for marginalized communities to express their voices and perspectives. 

We will delve into the various ways in which public art can be used to foster social inclusion, such as through community-based art projects, public art commissions, and art education programs. We will also examine the role of public art in promoting economic development, by attracting tourists, stimulating local economies, and creating job opportunities. 

Furthermore, we will discuss the challenges and opportunities associated with incorporating public art into local policies and strategies. This includes addressing issues of accessibility, representation, and sustainability, as well as leveraging the potential of public art to promote social cohesion and community resilience. 

Through this chapter, we aim to provide a comprehensive understanding of the role of public art in promoting social inclusion and economic development, and to equip readers with the knowledge and tools to effectively incorporate public art into their local policies and strategies.




### Introduction:

In this chapter, we will explore the intersection of arts planning and economic development in the context of creating a just city. The arts have long been recognized as a powerful tool for community building and revitalization, and their potential for economic growth and development is immense. However, the use of arts planning as a strategy for economic development is often overlooked or misunderstood. This chapter aims to shed light on the importance of arts planning in creating a vibrant and equitable city, and how it can be used as a tool for economic development.

We will begin by examining the role of arts planning in creating a just city. A just city is one that is inclusive, equitable, and promotes social and economic well-being for all its residents. The arts have the power to bring people together, foster a sense of community, and promote social cohesion. By incorporating arts planning into local policies and strategies, cities can create a more inclusive and equitable environment for all residents.

Next, we will delve into the economic impacts of arts planning. The arts have been shown to have a significant impact on the economy, both at the local and national level. By supporting and promoting the arts, cities can create jobs, attract tourists, and stimulate economic growth. We will explore the various ways in which arts planning can be used as a tool for economic development, and how it can benefit both the arts community and the overall economy.

Finally, we will discuss the challenges and opportunities of arts planning for economic development. We will examine these challenges and discuss potential solutions and strategies for overcoming them.

By the end of this chapter, readers will have a better understanding of the role of arts planning in creating a just city and its potential for economic development. We hope that this chapter will serve as a valuable resource for policymakers, urban planners, and anyone interested in using the arts as a tool for creating a more vibrant and equitable city.




#### Conclusion

### Introduction

In this chapter, we will explore the complex relationship between commercial development and commercial values in the neighborhood. Commercial development plays a crucial role in shaping the economic landscape of a neighborhood, and it is influenced by a variety of factors, including local policies and community values. Understanding this relationship is essential for creating equitable and inclusive neighborhoods that meet the needs and aspirations of all residents.

We will begin by examining the role of local policies in shaping commercial development. Local policies, such as zoning regulations and tax incentives, can influence the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in a neighborhood and the amount of space they are allocated. These policies can also impact the affordability of commercial space, which in turn affects the types of businesses that can afford to operate in the neighborhood.

Next, we will delve into the concept of commercial values and how they shape commercial development. Commercial values refer to the beliefs, attitudes, and behaviors that guide how businesses operate and interact with the community. These values can range from profit-driven to community-oriented, and they can have a significant impact on the types of businesses that are attracted to a neighborhood.

Finally, we will explore the relationship between commercial development and community values. Commercial development can both reflect and shape community values. On one hand, commercial development can reflect the values of the community, as businesses are often tailored to meet the needs and preferences of the residents. On the other hand, commercial development can also shape community values, as businesses can influence the way residents perceive and interact with their neighborhood.

By the end of this chapter, readers will have a better understanding of the complex dynamics between commercial development and commercial values in the neighborhood. This knowledge will be crucial for policymakers, community leaders, and businesses in creating equitable and inclusive neighborhoods that meet the needs and aspirations of all residents.




### Subsection: 10.1a Neighborhood Commercial Development

Commercial development in a neighborhood is a complex process that is influenced by a variety of factors. These factors include local policies, community values, and the physical characteristics of the neighborhood. In this section, we will explore the role of local policies in shaping commercial development in the neighborhood.

#### Local Policies and Commercial Development

Local policies play a crucial role in shaping commercial development in a neighborhood. These policies can influence the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in a neighborhood, the amount of space they are allocated, and the affordability of commercial space. For example, zoning regulations can restrict the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in certain areas, while tax incentives can make commercial space more affordable for businesses.

One of the key local policies that can impact commercial development is the inclusionary zoning policy. This policy requires a certain percentage of affordable housing units in new developments, which can help to address the issue of gentrification and displacement in neighborhoods. By promoting affordable housing, inclusionary zoning can also attract a diverse range of businesses to a neighborhood, as it allows for a more diverse and inclusive customer base.

Another important policy is the commercial rent subsidy. This policy provides financial assistance to businesses, particularly small businesses, to help offset the costs of commercial rent. By making commercial space more affordable, this policy can encourage more businesses to locate in a neighborhood, which can in turn stimulate economic growth and revitalization.

#### Commercial Values and Commercial Development

Commercial values also play a significant role in shaping commercial development in a neighborhood. These values refer to the beliefs, attitudes, and behaviors that guide how businesses operate and interact with the community. They can range from profit-driven to community-oriented, and they can have a significant impact on the types of businesses that are attracted to a neighborhood.

For example, businesses with a strong commitment to social responsibility and sustainability may be more likely to locate in a neighborhood with similar values. This can help to create a sense of community and belonging, as well as contribute to the overall well-being of the neighborhood.

#### The Relationship between Commercial Development and Community Values

The relationship between commercial development and community values is complex and multifaceted. Commercial development can both reflect and shape community values. On one hand, commercial development can reflect the values of the community, as businesses are often tailored to meet the needs and preferences of the residents. On the other hand, commercial development can also shape community values, as businesses can influence the way residents perceive and interact with their neighborhood.

For example, the development of a new shopping center or retail district can bring new businesses and job opportunities to a neighborhood, which can improve the overall economic well-being of the community. However, it can also lead to changes in the character and identity of the neighborhood, which may not align with the values of some residents.

In conclusion, commercial development in a neighborhood is influenced by a variety of factors, including local policies and community values. By understanding and addressing these factors, we can create more equitable and inclusive neighborhoods that meet the needs and aspirations of all residents.





### Subsection: 10.1b Factors Influencing Commercial Values

Commercial values are shaped by a variety of factors, including local policies, community values, and the physical characteristics of the neighborhood. These factors can influence the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in a neighborhood, the amount of space they are allocated, and the affordability of commercial space.

#### Local Policies and Commercial Values

Local policies play a crucial role in shaping commercial values in a neighborhood. These policies can influence the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in certain areas, the amount of space they are allocated, and the affordability of commercial space. For example, zoning regulations can restrict the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in certain areas, while tax incentives can make commercial space more affordable for businesses.

One of the key local policies that can impact commercial values is the inclusionary zoning policy. This policy requires a certain percentage of affordable housing units in new developments, which can help to address the issue of gentrification and displacement in neighborhoods. By promoting affordable housing, inclusionary zoning can also attract a diverse range of businesses to a neighborhood, as it allows for a more diverse and inclusive customer base.

Another important policy is the commercial rent subsidy. This policy provides financial assistance to businesses, particularly small businesses, to help offset the costs of commercial rent. By making commercial space more affordable, this policy can encourage more businesses to locate in a neighborhood, which can in turn stimulate economic growth and revitalization.

#### Community Values and Commercial Values

Community values also play a significant role in shaping commercial values in a neighborhood. These values refer to the beliefs, attitudes, and behaviors that guide how businesses operate and interact with the community. For example, a community that values sustainability and environmental responsibility may attract businesses that align with these values, such as organic food stores or renewable energy companies.

Community values can also influence the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in a neighborhood. For instance, a community that values family-friendly environments may restrict the types of businesses that serve alcohol or have late-night hours. This can impact the types of businesses that are able to thrive in the neighborhood.

#### Physical Characteristics of the Neighborhood

The physical characteristics of a neighborhood can also influence commercial values. For example, the location of a neighborhood can impact the types of businesses that are able to operate there. A neighborhood located in a busy downtown area may attract more office buildings and retail stores, while a neighborhood located in a more residential area may attract more service-based businesses.

The physical characteristics of a neighborhood can also impact the affordability of commercial space. For instance, a neighborhood with a high cost of living may have more expensive commercial rent, making it more difficult for small businesses to operate. This can lead to a concentration of larger, more established businesses in the neighborhood.

In conclusion, commercial values in a neighborhood are shaped by a variety of factors, including local policies, community values, and the physical characteristics of the neighborhood. These factors can influence the types of businesses that are allowed to operate in a neighborhood, the amount of space they are allocated, and the affordability of commercial space. Understanding these factors is crucial for promoting a diverse and inclusive commercial landscape in a neighborhood.





### Subsection: 10.1c Strategies for Promoting Commercial Development

Promoting commercial development in a neighborhood requires a multi-faceted approach that addresses both local policies and community values. Here are some strategies that can be used to promote commercial development in a neighborhood:

#### Leveraging Local Policies

Local policies can be leveraged to promote commercial development. For instance, inclusionary zoning policies can be expanded to include commercial spaces, requiring a certain percentage of affordable commercial spaces in new developments. This can help to attract a diverse range of businesses to a neighborhood, providing more opportunities for local residents and stimulating economic growth.

Commercial rent subsidies can also be increased or expanded to more businesses, making commercial space more affordable and encouraging more businesses to locate in a neighborhood. Additionally, local governments can provide other incentives, such as tax breaks or grants, to attract businesses to a neighborhood.

#### Promoting Community Values

Promoting community values can also be an effective strategy for promoting commercial development. This can be achieved by encouraging businesses to adopt practices that align with the community's values. For example, if a community values sustainability, local governments can incentivize businesses to adopt sustainable practices, such as using renewable energy sources or implementing waste reduction programs.

Community engagement can also be used to promote community values. Local governments can organize events or workshops to educate businesses about the community's values and how they can align with them. This can help to create a sense of shared responsibility and commitment to the community among businesses, leading to more positive relationships and a stronger sense of community.

#### Collaborating with Existing Businesses

Collaborating with existing businesses can also be an effective strategy for promoting commercial development. This can involve working with existing businesses to identify opportunities for growth and expansion, or providing support and resources to help them thrive. By collaborating with existing businesses, local governments can help to create a more vibrant and diverse commercial landscape in a neighborhood.

In conclusion, promoting commercial development in a neighborhood requires a comprehensive approach that addresses local policies, community values, and existing businesses. By leveraging local policies, promoting community values, and collaborating with existing businesses, local governments can create a more thriving and inclusive commercial landscape in their neighborhoods.

### Conclusion

In this chapter, we have explored the complex relationship between commercial development and commercial values in the neighborhood. We have seen how commercial development can have both positive and negative impacts on a neighborhood, and how these impacts can be influenced by the values and policies of the local community. We have also discussed various strategies for promoting commercial development that align with the values of the community, and for mitigating potential negative impacts.

Commercial development is a crucial aspect of economic development and the just city. It provides opportunities for job creation, economic growth, and improved quality of life. However, it also presents challenges, such as gentrification, displacement, and changes in the character of the neighborhood. Therefore, it is essential for local governments and communities to carefully consider and manage commercial development to ensure that it benefits all members of the community.

In conclusion, commercial development and commercial values are intertwined and require careful consideration and management. By understanding the complexities of this relationship and implementing effective strategies, we can create more equitable and inclusive neighborhoods that support economic development and the just city.

## Chapter: Chapter 11: Public Space Design and Public Space Values

### Introduction

Public spaces are the heart of any community, serving as the physical manifestation of the social, cultural, and economic life of its inhabitants. They are the places where people gather, interact, and engage in various activities, from leisurely strolls to vibrant street markets. However, the design of these public spaces can significantly influence their value and impact on the community. This chapter, "Public Space Design and Public Space Values," delves into the intricate relationship between the design of public spaces and the values they embody.

The design of public spaces is a multifaceted process that involves a careful consideration of various factors, including the physical characteristics of the space, the needs and preferences of the community, and the broader socio-economic context. It is a process that requires a deep understanding of the values that the community ascribes to these spaces. These values can be diverse and complex, encompassing everything from aesthetic appeal and functionality to inclusivity and sustainability.

In this chapter, we will explore the various aspects of public space design, from the initial planning stages to the final implementation. We will also delve into the concept of public space values, examining how these values are shaped by the design of the space and how they, in turn, influence the design process. We will also discuss the role of local policy in shaping public space design and values, and how these policies can be used to promote equity and inclusion in the design of public spaces.

By the end of this chapter, readers should have a comprehensive understanding of the complex interplay between public space design and public space values. They should also be equipped with the knowledge and tools to effectively navigate the challenges and opportunities that arise in the design of public spaces, and to create spaces that are not only aesthetically pleasing and functional, but also inclusive and equitable.




#### Conclusion

In this chapter, we have explored the complex relationship between commercial development and commercial values in the neighborhood. We have seen how the rise of commercialization has transformed the landscape of many neighborhoods, bringing both opportunities and challenges. We have also discussed the importance of local policies and strategies in guiding commercial development towards a more equitable and inclusive direction.

Commercial development is a double-edged sword. On one hand, it can bring jobs, economic growth, and improved services to a neighborhood. On the other hand, it can also lead to gentrification, displacement, and the loss of local character. The key is to strike a balance and ensure that commercial development is inclusive and benefits all members of the community.

Local policies and strategies play a crucial role in shaping commercial development. They can set guidelines for the types of businesses allowed, the size and scale of development, and the provision of affordable housing. They can also incentivize developers to include affordable housing, public spaces, and other community benefits in their projects.

However, implementing these policies and strategies can be challenging. It requires collaboration and compromise among various stakeholders, including developers, community members, and government agencies. It also requires ongoing monitoring and adjustment to address emerging issues and changing circumstances.

In conclusion, commercial development and commercial values in the neighborhood are complex and multifaceted. They require careful consideration and management to ensure that they contribute to the creation of a just city where all members of the community have equal opportunities to thrive.

### Introduction

In the previous chapters, we have explored various aspects of economic development and the just city, focusing on the role of local policies and strategies. We have discussed the importance of equity and inclusion in these processes, and how they can be achieved through different means. In this chapter, we will delve deeper into the concept of social enterprise as a tool for development.

Social enterprise is a business model that prioritizes social and environmental impact over profit. It is a growing trend in the world of business, with more and more companies adopting this approach. In this chapter, we will explore the concept of social enterprise and its potential for economic development and the just city.

We will begin by defining social enterprise and discussing its key characteristics. We will then delve into the role of social enterprise in economic development, examining how it can be used as a tool for creating jobs, stimulating local economies, and promoting sustainable practices. We will also explore the potential of social enterprise in addressing social and environmental issues, and how it can contribute to creating a more just and inclusive city.

Furthermore, we will discuss the challenges and opportunities of social enterprise, including the potential for collaboration between social enterprises and traditional businesses. We will also examine the role of local policies and strategies in promoting and supporting social enterprise, and how they can be used to create a more conducive environment for social enterprises to thrive.

Overall, this chapter aims to provide a comprehensive understanding of social enterprise and its potential for economic development and the just city. By the end of this chapter, readers will have a better understanding of the concept of social enterprise and its role in creating a more equitable and inclusive society. 


## Chapter 11: Toward Control: Social Enterprise as Development:




### Section: 11.1a Social Enterprises and Economic Development

Social enterprises have gained significant attention in recent years as a potential solution to address economic development and create a more just city. In this section, we will explore the role of social enterprises in economic development and how they can contribute to creating a more equitable and inclusive society.

#### What is a Social Enterprise?

A social enterprise is a business model that prioritizes social and environmental impact over profit. It is a dynamic and adaptive approach that operates to achieve a balanced financial, social, and environmental set of objectives. Social enterprises are driven by a shared common thread of creating positive change in the world, and they achieve this by operating as a business.

Social enterprises can take various forms, including trading enterprises, worker- and employee-owned trading enterprises, and community enterprises. These enterprises operate with the goal of creating a positive impact on society and the environment, while also generating revenue. This revenue is then reinvested into the mission of the enterprise, creating a sustainable and long-term solution for economic development.

#### The Role of Social Enterprises in Economic Development

Social enterprises play a crucial role in economic development by addressing the needs of communities and individuals in an ever-changing world. They operate with the goal of creating a balanced financial, social, and environmental set of objectives, making them a valuable tool for creating a more just and inclusive city.

One of the key ways in which social enterprises contribute to economic development is by creating job opportunities. By providing employment opportunities, social enterprises not only address the issue of unemployment but also provide individuals with valuable skills and experience. This not only benefits the individuals but also contributes to the overall economic growth of the city.

Moreover, social enterprises also play a crucial role in stimulating local economies. By operating as businesses, they generate revenue and create a ripple effect in the local economy. This revenue is then reinvested into the mission of the enterprise, creating a sustainable and long-term solution for economic development.

#### Addressing Social and Environmental Issues

Social enterprises also play a significant role in addressing social and environmental issues. By prioritizing social and environmental impact, they are able to address the needs of marginalized communities and promote sustainable practices. This not only creates a positive impact on society and the environment but also contributes to creating a more just and inclusive city.

#### Collaboration and Local Policies

Collaboration between social enterprises and traditional businesses is crucial for the success of social enterprises. By working together, they can leverage their strengths and create a more significant impact. Local policies and strategies also play a crucial role in promoting and supporting social enterprises. By creating a conducive environment for social enterprises to thrive, local policies can contribute to the overall success of social enterprises in economic development.

In conclusion, social enterprises have the potential to play a significant role in economic development and creating a more just and inclusive city. By prioritizing social and environmental impact, creating job opportunities, and stimulating local economies, social enterprises are a valuable tool for addressing the needs of communities and individuals in an ever-changing world. Collaboration and local policies are crucial for the success of social enterprises, and by working together, we can create a more equitable and sustainable future for all.


## Chapter 11: Toward Control: Social Enterprise as Development:




#### 11.1b Models of Social Enterprise

There are various models of social enterprise that can be used to achieve economic development and create a more just and inclusive city. These models can be broadly categorized into three types: trading enterprises, worker- and employee-owned trading enterprises, and community enterprises.

##### Trading Enterprises

Trading enterprises are the most common type of social enterprise. They operate like any other business, but with a focus on creating a positive social and environmental impact. These enterprises generate revenue by selling goods or services to customers, and the profits are reinvested into the mission of the enterprise. Trading enterprises can range from small-scale operations to large corporations, and they can operate in any industry.

##### Worker- and Employee-Owned Trading Enterprises

Worker- and employee-owned trading enterprises are a type of social enterprise where the workers and employees have a stake in the ownership of the enterprise. This model promotes a sense of ownership and responsibility among the workers and employees, leading to increased motivation and productivity. These enterprises can also provide a more stable and secure employment for workers and employees, as they have a say in the decision-making process.

##### Community Enterprises

Community enterprises are social enterprises that are owned and operated by a community. These enterprises are often created to address the specific needs and challenges faced by a community, and they can take various forms, such as cooperatives, mutual organizations, or community interest companies. Community enterprises promote community empowerment and self-reliance, and they can also provide employment opportunities for community members.

#### The Role of Policy in Supporting Social Enterprises

Local policies play a crucial role in supporting and promoting social enterprises. These policies can provide incentives for businesses to adopt social enterprise models, such as tax breaks or grants. They can also create a supportive regulatory environment that allows social enterprises to thrive. Additionally, local policies can promote social procurement, where public institutions and organizations prioritize purchasing goods and services from social enterprises.

In conclusion, social enterprises are a valuable tool for economic development and creating a more just and inclusive city. By adopting different models of social enterprise and implementing supportive local policies, we can create a more equitable and sustainable future for all.





### Subsection: 11.1c Addressing Social Challenges through Social Enterprise

Social enterprises have the potential to address a wide range of social challenges, from poverty and unemployment to social exclusion and environmental degradation. By leveraging market-based approaches, social enterprises can create sustainable solutions to these challenges, while also promoting social and economic equity.

#### Social Challenges and Social Enterprises

Social enterprises can address social challenges in various ways. For instance, they can provide employment opportunities for marginalized communities, thereby reducing unemployment and poverty. They can also promote social inclusion by creating spaces for marginalized groups to participate in economic activities. Furthermore, social enterprises can contribute to environmental sustainability by adopting environmentally friendly practices and technologies.

#### Social Impact Assessment and Social Enterprises

Social impact assessment is a crucial tool for evaluating the social performance of social enterprises. It involves measuring the social, economic, and environmental impacts of a social enterprise's activities. This assessment can help social enterprises understand their strengths and weaknesses, and identify areas for improvement. It can also provide valuable information for stakeholders, including investors, customers, and policymakers.

#### Social Impact Assessment Methods

There are various methods for conducting social impact assessment. These include the Social Return on Investment (SROI) method, the Social Impact Assessment (SIA) method, and the Social Impact Bond (SIB) method. Each of these methods has its own strengths and limitations, and the choice of method depends on the specific context and objectives of the social enterprise.

#### Social Impact Assessment and Policy

Policy plays a crucial role in promoting and supporting social enterprises. Policies can provide incentives for businesses to adopt social en

This collaborative approach is particularly important in the context of economic development and the just city, where the challenges are complex and require a multifaceted response.

Finally, we have highlighted the importance of policy support and regulatory frameworks in fostering a conducive environment for social enterprises. Policies that promote social enterprise can help to create a level playing field for these organizations, enabling them to compete on an equal footing with traditional businesses. They can also provide incentives and support for social enterprises, encouraging their growth and impact.

### Introduction

In this chapter, we will be discussing the importance of public roundtables in the context of equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. Public roundtables are a crucial tool for engaging the community and stakeholders in a meaningful dialogue about the issues and challenges facing a city. They provide a platform for diverse perspectives to be heard and for solutions to be proposed and discussed. 

The chapter will explore the role of public roundtables in promoting equity and inclusion, and how they can be used to address the economic disparities and social inequalities that exist in many cities. We will also discuss the benefits of public roundtables, such as increased community engagement, improved understanding of complex issues, and the potential for innovative solutions. 

Furthermore, we will delve into the challenges and limitations of public roundtables, such as the potential for unequal representation and the need for careful facilitation. We will also provide practical tips and strategies for organizing and facilitating effective public roundtables.

It will provide readers with a comprehensive understanding of the role of public roundtables and how they can be used as a tool for positive change in their communities.




### Section: 12.1 Public Roundtable:

Public roundtables are a crucial tool for promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. They provide a platform for diverse perspectives to be heard and for solutions to be proposed and discussed. In this section, we will explore the importance and purpose of public roundtables in the context of equity and inclusion.

#### 12.1a Importance and Purpose of Public Roundtables

Public roundtables serve multiple purposes in promoting equity and inclusion. Firstly, they provide a space for diverse perspectives to be heard. In many cities, there are often disparities and inequalities that exist between different communities. Public roundtables allow for these communities to come together and have a dialogue about the issues that affect them. This not only promotes understanding and empathy, but also allows for the identification of potential solutions.

Secondly, public roundtables can be used to address economic disparities and social inequalities. By bringing together stakeholders from different backgrounds, roundtables can facilitate discussions about the root causes of these disparities and inequalities. This can lead to the development of policies and programs that aim to address these issues and promote equity.

Thirdly, public roundtables can also serve as a platform for community engagement. By involving community members in the decision-making process, roundtables can increase their sense of ownership and empowerment. This can lead to a more inclusive and participatory approach to economic development and the just city.

However, public roundtables also have their limitations. One of the main challenges is ensuring equal representation and participation. In many cases, marginalized communities may not have the resources or access to participate in these discussions. This can lead to unequal representation and hinder the effectiveness of roundtables.

To address these challenges, it is important to have careful facilitation and planning for public roundtables. This includes ensuring diverse representation, creating a safe and inclusive space for discussion, and providing resources and support for community members to participate. Additionally, it is important to follow up on the discussions and recommendations from roundtables to ensure action is taken.

In conclusion, public roundtables are a crucial tool for promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. They provide a platform for diverse perspectives to be heard, address economic disparities and social inequalities, and promote community engagement. However, careful planning and facilitation are necessary to ensure their effectiveness. 





#### 12.1b Organizing and Facilitating a Public Roundtable

Organizing and facilitating a public roundtable requires careful planning and consideration. The following are some key steps to consider when organizing a public roundtable:

1. Identify the purpose and goals of the roundtable: Before organizing a roundtable, it is important to clearly define the purpose and goals. This will help guide the selection of participants and the agenda for the roundtable.

2. Select participants: The success of a public roundtable depends on the diversity and representation of participants. It is important to invite a diverse group of stakeholders, including community members, government officials, and experts. This will ensure a well-rounded and comprehensive discussion.

3. Develop an agenda: The agenda for the roundtable should be developed in collaboration with the participants. It should include topics that are relevant to the purpose and goals of the roundtable, and should allow for open and respectful dialogue.

4. Facilitate the roundtable: The roundtable should be facilitated by a neutral and impartial moderator. The moderator should ensure that all participants have an equal opportunity to speak and that the discussion remains respectful and productive.

5. Document and follow up: It is important to document the discussions and outcomes of the roundtable. This can be done through notes, audio or video recordings, or a written report. Follow up with participants to address any concerns or next steps.

Public roundtables can be a powerful tool for promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. By carefully organizing and facilitating these discussions, we can create a space for diverse perspectives to be heard and for solutions to be proposed and implemented. 


#### 12.1c Case Studies of Public Roundtables

Public roundtables have been successfully implemented in various cities around the world, providing a platform for diverse perspectives to be heard and solutions to be proposed. In this section, we will explore some case studies of public roundtables and the impact they have had on promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city.

##### Case Study 1: The City of Boston, USA

The City of Boston, USA, has implemented a public roundtable called the "Boston Roundtable on Equity and Inclusion." This roundtable brings together community members, government officials, and experts to discuss and address issues of equity and inclusion in the city. The roundtable has been instrumental in identifying and addressing economic disparities and social inequalities in Boston. By providing a platform for diverse perspectives to be heard, the roundtable has been able to develop policies and programs that promote equity and inclusion in the city.

##### Case Study 2: The City of Cape Town, South Africa

The City of Cape Town, South Africa, has implemented a public roundtable called the "Cape Town Roundtable on Equity and Inclusion." This roundtable brings together community members, government officials, and experts to discuss and address issues of equity and inclusion in the city. The roundtable has been successful in promoting community engagement and participation in the decision-making process. By involving community members in the roundtable discussions, the city has been able to increase their sense of ownership and empowerment, leading to a more inclusive and participatory approach to economic development and the just city.

##### Case Study 3: The City of Barcelona, Spain

The City of Barcelona, Spain, has implemented a public roundtable called the "Barcelona Roundtable on Equity and Inclusion." This roundtable brings together community members, government officials, and experts to discuss and address issues of equity and inclusion in the city. The roundtable has been instrumental in promoting economic development and the just city by addressing economic disparities and social inequalities. By providing a platform for diverse perspectives to be heard, the roundtable has been able to develop policies and programs that promote equity and inclusion in the city.

These case studies demonstrate the effectiveness of public roundtables in promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. By bringing together diverse perspectives and promoting open dialogue, public roundtables can lead to the development of policies and programs that address economic disparities and social inequalities. They also provide a platform for community engagement and participation, leading to a more inclusive and participatory approach to economic development and the just city. 


### Conclusion
In this chapter, we have explored the importance of public roundtables in promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. We have discussed the benefits of bringing together diverse stakeholders to discuss and address issues of equity and inclusion, and how this can lead to more effective and sustainable solutions. We have also examined the role of local policies in shaping the outcomes of these roundtables, and how they can be used to create a more equitable and inclusive environment for all members of the community.

Through our discussion, we have seen that public roundtables provide a valuable platform for community members to voice their concerns and perspectives, and for policymakers to gain a better understanding of the needs and challenges faced by different groups. By fostering open and respectful dialogue, these roundtables can help bridge the gap between marginalized communities and the mainstream, and promote a sense of belonging and empowerment.

Furthermore, we have explored the role of local policies in shaping the outcomes of public roundtables. These policies can serve as a framework for addressing issues of equity and inclusion, and can guide the decision-making process in a way that promotes fairness and equality. By incorporating equity and inclusion considerations into local policies, we can create a more just and equitable city for all.

In conclusion, public roundtables and local policies are essential tools in promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. By bringing together diverse stakeholders and incorporating equity and inclusion considerations into local policies, we can create a more inclusive and equitable environment for all members of the community.

## Chapter: Equity & Inclusion: Local Policy-Driven Strategies for Economic Development & the Just City

### Introduction:

In today's rapidly changing world, the concept of equity and inclusion has become increasingly important in shaping the future of our cities. As we continue to face challenges such as economic inequality, social exclusion, and environmental degradation, it is crucial for local governments to implement policies and strategies that promote equity and inclusion in all aspects of economic development. This chapter will explore the role of local policy in creating a just city, where all members of the community have equal access to opportunities and resources.

The chapter will begin by defining key terms such as equity, inclusion, and economic development, and how they relate to each other. It will then delve into the various factors that contribute to economic inequality and social exclusion, and how local policies can address these issues. The chapter will also discuss the importance of community engagement and participation in the policy-making process, and how it can lead to more effective and sustainable solutions.

Furthermore, the chapter will examine the role of local policies in promoting economic development and creating a thriving city. This includes policies related to housing, education, employment, and healthcare, among others. It will also explore the potential benefits and challenges of implementing equity and inclusion policies, and how they can be addressed.

Finally, the chapter will conclude with a discussion on the future of equity and inclusion in local policy-making, and how it can shape the direction of economic development and the just city. It will also provide recommendations for local governments to consider when developing and implementing policies that promote equity and inclusion.

Overall, this chapter aims to provide a comprehensive understanding of the role of local policy in creating a just city, where all members of the community have equal opportunities to thrive and prosper. By promoting equity and inclusion, we can create a more inclusive and sustainable future for all.





#### 12.1c Analyzing and Implementing Public Roundtable Feedback

After a public roundtable has been organized and facilitated, it is crucial to analyze and implement the feedback received. This process involves reflecting on the discussions, identifying key themes and recommendations, and developing a plan for implementation.

##### Reflecting on the Discussions

The first step in analyzing and implementing public roundtable feedback is to reflect on the discussions that took place. This can be done by reviewing the notes, audio or video recordings, or written report from the roundtable. It is important to consider the perspectives and insights shared by each participant, as well as the overall tone and dynamics of the discussion.

##### Identifying Key Themes and Recommendations

Next, it is important to identify the key themes and recommendations that emerged from the discussions. This can be done by categorizing the feedback into common themes and prioritizing the recommendations based on their feasibility and potential impact. It is also important to consider the diversity of perspectives and ensure that all voices are represented in the final analysis.

##### Developing a Plan for Implementation

Once the key themes and recommendations have been identified, a plan for implementation can be developed. This plan should outline the specific actions that will be taken to address the feedback, as well as the timeline and resources needed for implementation. It is important to involve all stakeholders in this process to ensure buy-in and accountability.

##### Monitoring and Evaluating Progress

Finally, it is crucial to monitor and evaluate the progress of the implementation plan. This can be done through regular check-ins with stakeholders, as well as tracking the impact of the implemented changes. Adjustments can be made to the plan as needed to ensure its effectiveness.

By analyzing and implementing public roundtable feedback, cities can create a more equitable and inclusive environment for all residents. This process not only promotes transparency and accountability, but also fosters a sense of community ownership and empowerment. 


### Conclusion
In this chapter, we have explored the importance of public roundtables in promoting equity and inclusion in economic development and the just city. We have discussed the benefits of bringing together diverse stakeholders to discuss and address issues related to economic development, and how this can lead to more informed and effective decision-making. We have also highlighted the role of local policies in shaping the outcomes of these roundtables, and how they can be used to create a more equitable and inclusive environment for all members of the community.

Through the use of public roundtables, we have seen how local governments can foster a sense of community ownership and participation in economic development initiatives. By involving a diverse group of stakeholders, including community members, businesses, and non-profit organizations, these roundtables can provide a platform for open and honest dialogue, leading to more comprehensive and sustainable solutions. Additionally, by incorporating equity and inclusion principles into the policies and guidelines used in these roundtables, we can ensure that the needs and perspectives of marginalized and underrepresented groups are taken into account.

As we conclude this chapter, it is important to recognize that public roundtables are just one tool in the larger process of creating a more equitable and inclusive city. It is crucial for local governments to continue to prioritize and invest in initiatives that promote equity and inclusion, and to use public roundtables as a means of engaging and empowering the community in this process. By working together and utilizing local policies, we can create a more just and prosperous city for all.
